Practicing mindfulness involves breathing methods, guided imagery, and other practices to relax the body and mind and help reduce stress.\n\nSpending too much time planning, problem-solving, daydreaming, or thinking negative or random thoughts can be draining. {"summary": "Painful intercourse, also known as dyspareunia, is a symptom that can occur during perimenopause and menopause. In menopause, it is often caused by vaginal dryness due to the consistently low levels of estrogen. While many symptoms overlap between perimenopause and menopause, painful intercourse is a more stable and long-term issue associated with menopause. Menopause is defined as the permanent end of menstruation due to loss of ovarian function, typically confirmed after 12 consecutive months without a period. It occurs on average around age 51 in the U.S. and 49 in Brazil. During menopause, estrogen and progesterone levels remain consistently low, contributing to symptoms like hot flashes, night sweats, sleep disturbances, low libido, mood changes, memory issues, thinning hair, dry skin, weight gain, and an increased risk of osteoporosis and cardiovascular issues."}

During perimenopause, ovaries gradually produce less estrogen and progesterone, leading to fluctuating hormone levels and symptoms like irregular periods, hot flashes, mood swings, sleep problems, and fatigue. Menopause is diagnosed after 12 consecutive months without a period, with estrogen and progesterone levels remaining consistently low. Common menopausal symptoms include persistent hot flashes, vaginal dryness, low libido, and an increased risk of osteoporosis and cardiovascular issues."
